    a
    new
    mode
    to
    the
    freighter
    bot:
    the
    scavenger.

    The
    scavenger
    will
    warp
    to
    a
    belt
    bookmark,
    warp
    to
    a
    wreck,
    loot
    the
    wreck,
    and
    move
    on. It
    does
    not
    look
    for
    other
    player
    or
    NPC
    ships. NPC
    ships
    are
    usually
    not
    a
    problem
    because
    it
    will
    get
    in
    and
    out
    before
    they
    do
    any
    serious
    damage. Use
    a
    fast
    ship
    with
    a
    decent
    cargohold.

    For
    example,
    a
    Prober
    with
    a
    cargo
    extender,
    micro
    aux.
    power
    control,
    small
    shield
    extender,
    and
    medium
    shield
    extender
    seems
    to
    work
    well.
